        <div class="abstract anim">
         <div class="container">
          <h1>
           香港必遊旅遊景點 - 昂坪360
          </h1>
          <p>
           昂坪360被譽為世界十大最佳纜車體驗，提供一日遊及優惠套票選擇，讓你深度暢遊香港大嶼山！
          </p>
          <p class="hidden">
           昂坪纜車旅程，連接東涌至昂坪，令你飽覽香港大嶼山的優美景致。纜車一到達就是昂坪市集，也是前往天壇大佛、寶蓮禪寺、大澳漁村等香港必去景點的最佳方法。昂坪市集集休閒、購物、和四大主題景點於一身，是旅客及本地人假日遊的人氣熱點！
          </p>
          <a class="readmore visible-xs" href="#">
           <span>
            閱讀更多
           </span>
           <span class="sp sp-readmore">
           </span>
          </a>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="row anim shortcut-3-up">
         <div class="col col-md-4 col-xs-8">
          <div class="cb-01">
           <div class="ratio4-3 ratio">
            <a class="cover-img lazy" data-src="https://www.np360.com.hk/sites/default/files/homepage_shortcut/main_image/1806/09_tickets_%26_tours_360funpass_TC_800x600_0.jpg" href="https://www.np360.com.hk/tc/ticketing/tickets-tours/entertainment-package/360-fun-pass">
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="content">
            <div class="table-row">
             <h4>
              <a href="https://www.np360.com.hk/tc/ticketing/tickets-tours/entertainment-package/360-fun-pass">
               360娛樂套票
              </a>
             </h4>
            </div>
            <div class="table-row desc hidden-xs">
             <div class="wrap">
              <p>
               低至64折優惠，尊享來回纜車及一票暢遊昂坪市集三大主題景點。
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="table-row hidden-xs">
             <a class="viewmore" href="https://www.np360.com.hk/tc/ticketing/tickets-tours/entertainment-package/360-fun-pass">
              <svg enable-background="new 0 0 44 44" height="44px" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 44 44" width="44px" x="0px" xml:space="preserve" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:a="http://ns.adobe.com/AdobeSVGViewerExtensions/3.0/" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" y="0px">
               <defs>
               </defs>
               <circle class="border-hover" cx="22" cy="22" fill="none" r="21.5" stroke="#25A3DD" stroke-miterlimit="10" stroke-width="1.5">
               </circle>
